by this self whose single delight lies in belonging entirely to Him,
by its proper form, continuation, and activity controlled by Him,
and by the body, senses, and mindтАФ
now begins to bring about all enjoyments, such as are honorific, tangible, and pertaining to food, etc.,
such as are made of His innate and most auspicious substances,
such as are achieved with extreme devotion,
and such as are utterly resplendent, utterly complete, and most pleasing.
All these are for His own pleasure, for Himself along with all His retinue and insignia.тАЭ

and such as are made of His own innate and most auspicious substances,
such as are achieved with extreme devotion and are most pleasing, utterly complete, utterly resplendent.
All these are for His own pleasure, for Himself along with all His retinue and insignia.тАЭ37

FX Clooney

With mind, understanding, and ego,
he places on the ground
like a tortoise -
his four limbs and his head as a fifth.

Always with a rotation in that form,
he pays reverence with his eight limbs.
He pays respect with his eight limbs.
He sits before the all-pervading one.

Thus the eightfold obeisance is stated.

  1. paramaik─Бnti: тАЬthe person single-mindedly focused on the HighestтАЭ or perhaps, тАЬthe highest single minded person.тАЭ

    Krishna Ayyangar Swami offers this definition of the paramaik─Бnti:

    who does what is to be done (satkс╣Ыtya) purely from enjoyment, is the one solely focused on the highest and considered the best among the great devotees

    yas tu bhogatay─Б viс╣гс╣Зoс╕е
    satkс╣Ыtyaс╣Г kurute sad─Б
    sa eva paramaik─Бnt─л
    mah─Бbh─Бgavatottamaс╕е

    (2010: 15).

    He also offers two lower categories:

    • the Vaiс╣гс╣Зavas (devotees of Viс╣гс╣Зu who do what is to be done [nitya] and occasional [naimittika] as their means to pleasing the Lord) and
    • Vaiс╣гс╣Зavottamas (the highest devotees of Viс╣гс╣Зu who single-mindedly obey the commands of the Lord and do what is required).
     ↩︎
